unique[0x20:3] = unique[0x10:3] & 0xfc00
unique[0x40:1] = unique[0x20:3] == 0x0
unique[0x50:3] = unique[0x10:3] & 0xfc00
unique[0x70:1] = unique[0x50:3] == 0x800
unique[0x80:3] = unique[0x10:3] & 0xfc00
